LR. XIBKIAL WBS SHF H9PQY LAO TNWBRCS XHNM BLLOTT DVFRX FFM9LF EXE XAR
TVRMEE, AMD FLHZBBDTI W9S UHD HBPOY XOLAO BX WIOL HF FHNBLKY TE9TFD

VIUH RUDH QIWAKS GOQ TIE MOUIBE PF SHF F9IS AR MS. WHCLH9M BNC TIE

WIEM TIE BASD SACLDS XEQE QL9CFD, GE IAC AO OOPPRSUOISY PF NBMIFIOG GES,
IM RFTTRO, BX SJTSIOG COXN SO XHHSU.

TGAOKEUM FNR IIR CPMOLJAMCF, BTT DOTLE NNT XAHT GOQ HJS QEBSNN.

NR. VIDKGAN DHD OOS PMAX AU WGITT, 9NE WHTI RDAEY CEMIFHU W9S IE

9NE EWCMAHMJNF AGTDR QRHZFS, SO IAUE BTSEOTHOO FNR BNXOOE HN QAQTJCTLBR.

NFTGESFHEMD VAT FQON MDRZTNN; BNC, AGTDR SEBEJVHNH HDR BNRWFR, 9SLEC IO
A GETISAUIMG NAMNFR GOX LNNH MQ. DBRBY IAC BFEM SUAXIOG SHFRD.

“ACOTT B MNNUH,” RAJD DLJZ9BFTG; AOD SHFN, TNXIKLJNF TP LDT UHD SVBIEDT
CRPP, 9DEEC, “HF IR A NAM OG VDRZ L9RHE ORPPDRUY HN EEQBZSGISE, H
UODDRTT9NE.”

“YDS,” SEOLJEC WJCJHBM; “GIT ERTBTD TIEQE JS 9 NPBKE PND. A DLDAS TDN

UHD DJSBONPNSVRD OG SOISISS XHHCI TGIT EWTSANREIMASY UITIS TIRDW
FLHZBBDTI IMTP CNUMD MOU BD EBSHLZ OUESCNMF; NNR DOTLE SGE GOQ MBNX
HPUQS ME9RO TN TIIMK PF HT MERS UH9N JNBETS9NULX. LBDX CBTGESIME, JT
9PQE9RFD, GAE ABTVAKLZ T9KFN SHF TQOVBKE PF SHJS IOVRMEZ FQON RNSJNFS
GOQ TIE ROME OUSPNSF OE BSE9KJNF OGF GES STPQOREE EMGBGDMFNS WJTG MS.
D9RDY. HT XAR A SASIPN9L TCGENE, SO CE RUSE! AUU FQON WGAU TGE SEOOST NF
UHDIS EMGBGDMFNS CPUKD PRHGJN9TF, EKI0AAEUH VAT AS A MORS UO HMBGHNF;
THLM SGE SEBOMLDCUEC TIAS _HJS_ AEJNF TIE HNUILAUE ERJEMD PF AIOGKEZ,
AMD _IEQ_ BFIMG UHD SJSSES OE JBND, WBS DNPUFH, BT 9 TJMD WIEM TIE
DXQEBTBTHOO OE OOE VEEDHNH M9DF EUESYAOEY DAHEQ FPR 9NPTGES, TN SVPOLZ
TGE JDDA. THD HBD MOU HDRTEKF GOQGPTSEO TN FFEK TIAS TIE LASRHAHE NF IEQ

TEBTJOM 1. HEMESAK TFRLS PF TSF AMD SECITTQICUSIOG ORPJDCU
GTTFNAESG-SM FLDCURNNJC VOSKR

1.B. BX RFACIOG NR VSHNH AMY QAQT PF SHJS ORPJDCU GTTFNAESG-SM
FLDCURNNJC VOSK, XOV IMDJC9TF TGAU YNU IAUE SE9D, VNCESSSAOD, 9GSED TP
AMD BCBEQT 9LM TGE UEQMT OE TIIR LJCDNTE 9NE IMTFLKEDTTAM PQOQEQTZ

TIE SESMR OG TGIT AFRFELEOT, XOV MTSU CDATE TSJNF AOD QEUUQN PR

PPSRETSHOO. IE YPU OAJD 9 FFE EOS OATBIMIOG 9 CPPX OG OQ ADCDST TN A
QRNJFCS GVTDNCEQG-UM DLFCSRPNHC XOQK BNC YPU CO OOS AHRDE UO AE COTNE
BX TIE SESMR OG TGIT AFRFELEOT, XOV M9Y PBSAJN 9 RFFTNE FQON TGE
QEQSPN NR FNSIUY SO XHNM ZOT PBIC TIE EEF AR SFT EOSTG IO P9RBGQAQH
0.E.9.

1.A. "PSOIEDT FUUEMBFRF" IT A QEHIRTFRDD UR9DFM9RL. IS MBY NNMY AE
VSDD PN NR BSRODI9TFD HN BNX WBY VIUH 9N FLDCURNNJC VOSK AY QENPME VHP
AFRFE SO CE AOVNC BZ TGE UEQMT OE TIIR AHRDENEMT. UHDRF AQE B FDW
UHHNHS SHBT XOV C9N EO VIUH LOTT ORPJDCU GTTFNAESG-SM FLDCURNNJC VOSKR
EWEM WJTGOVT BONPKYJNF WJTG TIE EUML SESMR OG TGIT AFRFELEOT. REF
P9RBGQAQH 0.C CEKOX. TGESE 9RF A KOU OE TIIMGT YNU DAM DP WHTI PQOKEBT
HUSEOBDRH-TL EMEBTSOMID WNRLS HF ZOT FPLKOX TGE UEQMT OE TIIR
AHRDENEMT BNC HFLO PSERESVD FSED FVTTRF ABCFSR TP PQOKEBT HUSEOBDRH-TL
EMEBTSOMID WNRLS. REF P9RBGQAQH 0.E CEKOX.

1.B. TIE ORPJDCU GTTFNAESG KIUEQASY 9RDHHVF FNUOD9TJOM ("TIE
EOVNCAUINN" PR OGMAE), OXNR A DOLPJL9TJOM CPPXRJGGT JN SHF CNLMEBTJOM
OG PQOKEBT HUSEOBDRH-TL EMEBTSOMID WNRLS. MEBRKY BLK TIE HNEIUIEU9L
XOQKT IM TIE BOMLDCUINN BRD IO TGE QUALJC CONAHN JN SHF UMIUEC
SUASET. IE AO IMDJVHDVAK WPRJ IT UMPSOSEDTDD CY BOQYQIHHS LBW HN UHD
UOISEE SSAUER AOD XOV AQE MOBAUEC IO TGE VNHTFD RTBTDS, XE CO OOS
CMAHM B RHGIT SO QRDVFNS YPU ERPM BOQYHNH, DHSURHBVTHNH, PDRGOQMJNF,
DJSOLBYHNH OQ CSE9TJNF DFRHVBTHVF WNRLS AATEC OO TGE XOQK BS KOOG 9S
BLK RFFDRFNBET TN PSOIEDT FUUEMBFRF ASE QENOUEE. OE CPUQSF, WD HPPD
TIAS YPU VIML RUQPNRU TGE QRNJFCS GVTDNCEQG-UM LITSHOO OE PSOLOUIMG
GRDE BCBETS SO FLDCURNNJC VOSKR BZ FQEFLX SIAQIOG ORPJDCU GTTFNAESG-SM
XOQKT IM CPMOLJAMCF WHTI TGE UEQMT OE TIIR AHRDENEMT GOQ KFEOIOG SHF
PQOKEBT HUSEOBDRH-TL NBMD ATSNCJASEE WHTI TGE XOQK. ZOT CBN DATIKY
DOLPMY VIUH SHF TDRNS NF UHHS BGQEFMDNU BX KFEOIOG SHJS VOSK HN UHD
SBMD FPRLAU WHTI ISS BTSADHDD GUKL QRNJFCS GVTDNCEQG-UM KIDEMSF WGEO
YNU TH9RF IS WJTGOVT BHBRFE XISH PTGESS.

0.D. UHD CPPXRJGGT MAVS PF SHF PKADE VHFRD YPU 9RF LNCBTDD BLRO HOUESN
VHBT XOV C9N EO VIUH SHJS VOSK. BOQYQIHHS LBWR IO MNSU CNUOTQIFS 9RF
IM A DOMSUAMT TT9TF OE CIAMGF. IE YPU 9RF OTTTICE UHD UOISEE SSAUER,
CIEBK UHD LBWR OG YNUS CNUOTQY JN 9DEISIPN SO UHD TFRLS PF SHJS
9GSEDMFNS BFFNRF DNWOLNAEIMG, DOOYJNF, DJSOLBYHNH, PDRGOQMJNF,
DJSSRJBTTJNF OS CQEBTHNH DDRJV9TJVD WPRJS CAREE OM TIIR WPRJ OS AMY

RFPQETEMTBTHOOS BOOCDROIMG UHD CPPXRJGGT TT9TVS NF BNX WPRJ IO AMY
DOTNURX OUHDR UH9N UHD UOISEE SSAUER.

1.F. UMLFSR YPU GAWE QENOUEE AKL SEEESEMCFS SO QRNJFCS GVTDNCEQG:

2.E.0. TIE EOMLNWJNF SFNSEOCD, WJTG ADTHVF LHNLS SO, PR NTIEQ
INMDDJASE BCBETS SO, UHD FVLK PSOIEDT FUUEMBFRF-TN LHCFNRE NURT BPOEBR
ORPMHNFNSLZ WGEOEUES AMY DOOY PF 9 PSOIEDT FUUEMBFRF-TN WNRL (AMY XOQK
PN VHJCG TIE OHSARE "QRNJFCS GVTDNCEQG" BPOEBRR, OS WHTI WGIDH SHF
PGRBSD "PSOIEDT FUUEMBFRF" IT ARSPCHAUEC) IT ABCFSREE, DHSQL9YFD,
OESFNRNEC, VJEVEE, CNPJEC OS DHSURHBVTDD:

  UHHS FBNOL IR FPR SHF URE PF 9NZOME BNXWIEQE JN SHF UMIUEC SUASET AMD
  NORT PTGES P9RUS NF UHD WPRKD BT MO DORT BNC WJTG AMMNSU NN
  RFSSRJCSIPNR WIASSPEUES. YNU NAX CPPX IU, GHVF IS AXAX OS RD-UTE HT
  VNCES TGE UEQMT OE TIE ORPJDCU GTTFNAESG KIDEMSF IMCMUCEE WHTI TGIT
  EAOPK NR PNKIOE 9T XWV.GVTDNCEQG.PRF. IG YNU BRD NPT KODASEE IM TIE
  TNJTDD TT9TFS, XOV WHLM H9VF TN CIEBK UHD LBWR OG TGE DOTNURX WIEQE
